NOTE: This is a single output file from running AraSim with 100,000 neutrinos. I ran 29 of these jobs and copied one of the files to this file, replacing the effective volume (both ice and water) with the average value for each from the entire set of runs (2.9 million neutrinos). Thus, while this only indicates 100,000 neutrinos being thrown, it represents the entire 2.9 million neutrino results.
